/midico.db
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'paths' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL, 'path' TEXT UNIQUE )
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'performers' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL, 'nick' TEXT, 'first' TEXT, 'last' TEXT, 'sts' INTEGER, 'ss' INTEGER, 'sdone' INTEGER, 'email' TEXT, 'pass' TEXT, 'lang' TEXT, 'priv' INTEGER )
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'music' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL , 'artist' TEXT, 'title' TEXT, 'file' TEXT UNIQUE, 'format' INTEGER, 'lyr' INTEGER, 'uniqueid' TEXT, 'share' INTEGER, 'fcheck' INTEGER, 'cat' INTEGER, 'rt_sum' INTEGER, 'rt_num' INTEGER )
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'tperf' ('idp' INTEGER UNIQUE, 'left' INTEGER, 'done' INTEGER, 'dt' DATETIME )
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'turns' ('ids' INTEGER,'nick' TEXT,'artist' TEXT,'title' TEXT,'comm' TEXT,'file' TEXT, 'fmt' TEXT, 'turn' INTEGER,'dt' INTEGER,'force' INTEGER,'done' INTEGER, 'idsong' INTEGER, 'id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'competition' ('nick' TEXT,'title' TEXT,'artist' TEXT,'comm' TEXT,'scores' TEXT,'total' INTEGER,'file' TEXT, 'id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'favourites' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL, 'ids' INTEGER, 'idsong' INTEGER, 'rate' INTEGER , 'pitch' INTEGER DEFAULT 0)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'playlists' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT NOT NULL, 'name' TEXT, 'flag' INTEGER, 'pause' INTEGER)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS 'pldata' ('id' INTEGER PRIMARY KEY NOT NULL, 'idp' INTEGER, 'idl' INTEGER, 'title' TEXT, 'artist' TEXT, 'settings' TEXT, 'file' TEXT, 'ord' INTEGER DEFAULT (0) not null, 'status' INTEGER DEFAULT (0), 'fmt' TEXT)

uploadadv
Upload Titles
This function will upload all your song's title to Midico database. Only the title, the artist and the file signature will be trasmitted, no other informations about your file and, of course, none of your files will be uploaded.
Please check the accuracy of information on the songs. And please check the format for the Artist's name as follow:
Last name, first name ( if applicable, i.e. Morissette, Alanis ) 
Band name ( i.e. Pink Floyd and not Floyd, Pink )
